/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[ListarCiudades]    Script Date: 03/03/2014 05:32:40 p.m. ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[ListarCiudades]
	@codDepartamento int
AS
SELECT        id, nombre, departamento_id
FROM            localidades
WHERE        (departamento_id = @codDepartamento)

GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[ListarDepartamentos]    Script Date: 03/03/2014 05:32:40 p.m. ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[ListarDepartamentos]
	@codProvincia int
AS
SELECT        id, provincia_id, nombre
FROM            departamentos
WHERE        (provincia_id = @codProvincia)

GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[ListarProvincias]    Script Date: 03/03/2014 05:32:40 p.m. ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[ListarProvincias]
AS
SELECT        id, nombre
FROM            provincias

GO
